19.20(1): shon lhab lhub kyi na bza' sku la gsol/ glu gar rol mo sna tshogs kyis mdun bsus/
19.21(1): me tog bsil ba'i lding khang gi dbus su/ rin po che sna bdun gyi khri la bteg ste/
20.1(1): lha ye srid 'phrul gyi rgyal po zhes kyang bya/ lha'i dbang po brgya byin zhes bya bas/ lha mo 
20.2(1): de la mtshan gsol ba/ma bsrid ye srid srid pa'i lha mo yum/ sum cu rtsa gsum 
20.3(1): lha'i gnas na 'khrungs/ bag chags sred len mngal gyi dri ma med/ sku lus mtshan 
20.4(1): dpe lha mo yum du bstan/rigs bzang khungs btsun mkha' klong dag pa'i rgyud/
20.5(1): bzang za ring btsun sku la phyag 'tshal lo/ /lha khams gsal ba'i sgron ma 'deg tu 
20.6(1): gsol/ bstan pa rin chen rab tu bstan par mdzod/ lha mo khyod kyi cho 'brang ci 
20.7(1): ltar lags/ bdag cag rnams la nges pa'i bka' stsol cig /ces gsol bas/ lha

20.14(1): snod/ dbang po skye 'gro nang gi bcud/ tshogs brgyad 'dod yon mngon par spyod/

20.18(1): yul/ skra mtshams mgon btsun phywa yi grong / dung khang bar lha 'od gsal gnas/

20.21(1): lha rigs drug gnas/ rtsa chen dpag bsam ljon pa shing / rtsa phran lo 'dab bsil 
21.1(1): g.yab 'beb/ tsi ta rnam par rgyal ba gnas/ glo ba mtshal ri lha'i mdun/ mchin 
21.2(1): pa ar mo li ka'i rdo/ mchin dri yid 'ong mdzes pa'i tshal/ 'khris pa gling dgu 
21.3(1): 'khyil ba'i mtsho/ mtsher pa rtsub 'gyur dregs dang 'dres/ mkhal ma rin chen gling 
21.4(1): dang khrod/ srog rtsa ud dum wa ra'i tshal/ ol khang shel gyi cog chen des/ pho ba 
21.5(1): 'dod pa dgu 'gyur gling / yan lag gling bzhi gling phran brgyad/ rgyu ma mtha'i 
21.6(1): lcags ri 'khor/ spyan ni nyi zla gsal ba'i sgron/ snyan ni 'byung ba rtsa grang sgra/

21.11(1): rgya gram rlung / sku stod yan chad mtho ris gsum/ sku smad man chad ngan song gsum/
21.12(1): thams cad lha mo'i sku la rdzogs/ bzhed na 'jig rten bde ba ldan/ dgyes na stong 
21.13(1): gsum dga' ba skyed/ 'khros na khams gsum sgrol bar byed/ theg pa rim dgu zil 
21.14(1): gyis gnon/ khams gsum sa dgu dbang du sdud/ snang srid 'khor lo phyag gis

22.1(1): byad/ dpag tu med pa phul nas/ lha'i bu mo yod de rgyal bas/ mgrin pa'i gsang

23.1(1): sgrogs su bcugs/ sgo lnga'i yul las dbang po'i bran 'khor bskor/ tshogs brgyad
